          (chn_mixer): ChannelMixer(
            (mix): Sequential(
              (0): Linear(in_features=8, out_features=16, bias=True)
              (1): SiLU()
              (2): Linear(in_features=16, out_features=8, bias=True)
            )
          )
        )
      )
      (norm): RMSNorm((8,), eps=1e-06, elementwise_affine=True)
    )
  )
  (decoder): Transformer(
    (x_embedder): Sequential(
      (0): Linear(in_features=8, out_features=512, bias=True)
      (1): MLPMixer(
        (blocks): ModuleList(
          (0-1): 2 x MixerBlock(
            (norm1): RMSNorm((512,), eps=1e-06, elementwise_affine=True)
            (tok_mixer): TokenMixer(
              (mix): Sequential(
                (0): Linear(in_features=256, out_features=256, bias=True)
                (1): SiLU()
                (2): Linear(in_features=256, out_features=256, bias=True)
              )
            )
            (norm2): RMSNorm((512,), eps=1e-06, elementwise_affine=True)
            (chn_mixer): ChannelMixer(
              (mix): Sequential(
                (0): Linear(in_features=512, out_features=1024, bias=True)
                (1): SiLU()
                (2): Linear(in_features=1024, out_features=512, bias=True)
              )
            )
          )
        )
        (norm): RMSNorm((512,), eps=1e-06, elementwise_affine=True)
      )
    )
    (y_embedder): LabelEmbedder(
      (embedding_table): Embedding(11, 512)
    )
    (blocks): ModuleList(
      (0-7): 8 x Block(
        (norm1): RMSNorm((512,), eps=1e-06, elementwise_affine=True)
        (norm2): RMSNorm((512,), eps=1e-06, elementwise_affine=True)
        (attn): Attention(
          (qkv): Linear(in_features=512, out_features=1536, bias=True)
          (proj): Linear(in_features=512, out_features=512, bias=True)
        )
        (mlp): SwiGLUFFN(
          (w12): Linear(in_features=512, out_features=2730, bias=True)
          (w3): Linear(in_features=1365, out_features=512, bias=True)
        )
        (adaLN_modulation): Sequential(
          (0): SiLU()
          (1): Linear(in_features=512, out_features=3072, bias=True)
        )
      )
    )
    (ffn): ModulatedLinear(
      (linear): Linear(in_features=512, out_features=32, bias=True)
      (norm): RMSNorm((512,), eps=1e-06, elementwise_affine=True)
      (adaLN_modulation): Sequential(
        (0): SiLU()
        (1): Linear(in_features=512, out_features=1024, bias=True)
      )
    )
    (out): Sequential(
      (0): Rearrange('b (h w) c -> b c h w', h=16, w=16)
      (1): Contiguous()
      (2): Conv2d(32, 32, kernel_size=(3, 3), stride=(1, 1), padding=(1, 1), padding_mode=reflect)
      (3): SiLU()
      (4): ConvTranspose2d(32, 3, kernel_size=(4, 4), stride=(2, 2), padding=(1, 1))
      (5): Tanh()
    )
  )
)
